zvbi: electron gun to move back up to the first line of the television
zvbi: screen to trace the next screen field. The vertical blanking interval
zvbi: can be used to carry data, since anything sent during the VBI would
zvbi: naturally not be displayed; various test signals, closed captioning,
zvbi: and other digital data can be sent during this time period.
zvbi:
